# Text Elements
A small ball with a mass of 1.6 kg is thrown with an initial velocity < 6, 2, 0 > m/s at time 
t = 0 at a location we choose to call the origin < 0, 0, 0 >. Air resistance is negligible. 
The next few questions, A though I relate to this question.

    a. When the ball reaches its maximum height, what is its velocity vector? ^5SePm3P8

b. When the ball reaches its max height, what is t? ^lWU5Abhz
